[*Click here for event information on the Regional Pro Tour Qualifiers for Pro Tour Aether Revolt.*](http://magic.wizards.com/en/events/instoreplay/rptqaer)


Invitations to the Regional Pro Tour Qualifiers for Pro Tour *Aether Revolt* are awarded in the following manner:


* Winners of Preliminary Pro Tour Qualifiers tied to Regional Pro Qualifiers for Pro Tour *Aether Revolt* (held July 23, 2016 – October 9, 2016)
* Winners of Regional Last Chance Qualifiers that immediately precede each Regional Pro Tour Qualifier
* Players with a Pro Tour Players Club Silver level as of the date of the Regional Pro Tour Qualifier
* Players that finished 1st- through 8th- place in a Regional Pro Tour Qualifier from the Regional Pro Tour Qualifiers tied to Pro Tour *Kaladesh*.

If you believe that your finish at a Preliminary Pro Tour Qualifier is in error, please visit [www.wizards.com/Magic/PlaneswalkerPoints](http://www.wizards.com/Magic/PlaneswalkerPoints). After logging in, click the "Appeals Form" link at the bottom of the page and fill out the form.


This list is updated every Wednesday to account for adjustments and player appeals.


The following players are invited to compete in one Regional Pro Tour Qualifier for Pro Tour *Aether Revolt*:


***NOTE: This list is not final and subject to change at any time.***
